--
-- Table structure for table `employees`
--

CREATE TABLE `employees` (
  `id` varchar(5) NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `email` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `phone` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `office_id` int(5) NOT NULL,
  `updated_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` datetime DEFAULT current_timestamp()
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_general_ci;

--
-- Table structure for table `users`
--

CREATE TABLE `users` (
  `id` int(5) UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `email` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `password` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `employee_id` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `updated_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` datetime DEFAULT current_timestamp()
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 COLLATE=utf8_general_ci;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Stand-in structure for view `v_current_weak_performance`
-- (See below for the actual view)
--
CREATE TABLE `v_current_weak_performance` (
`order_count` bigint(21)
,`order_amount` decimal(65,0)
);

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Stand-in structure for view `v_recent_order`
-- (See below for the actual view)
--
CREATE TABLE `v_recent_order` (
`id` int(5)
,`employee_id` varchar(100)
,`employee_name` varchar(100)
,`employee_email` varchar(100)
,`employee_phone` varchar(100)
,`office_name` varchar(100)
,`order_date` datetime
,`order_item` varchar(100)
,`order_amount` int(100)
,`client_id` varchar(10)
,`client_name` varchar(100)
,`client_email` varchar(100)
,`client_phone` varchar(100)
);

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Stand-in structure for view `v_sales_performance`
-- (See below for the actual view)
--
CREATE TABLE `v_sales_performance` (
`id` varchar(5)
,`name` varchar(100)
,`count` bigint(21)
);

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Stand-in structure for view `v_total_income`
-- (See below for the actual view)
--
CREATE TABLE `v_total_income` (
`total_order` decimal(65,0)
,`total_order_last_month` decimal(65,0)
,`curr_month` int(2)
,`curr_year` int(4)
);

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Stand-in structure for view `v_total_order`
-- (See below for the actual view)
--
CREATE TABLE `v_total_order` (
`total_order` bigint(21)
,`total_order_last_month` bigint(21)
,`curr_month` int(2)
,`curr_year` int(4)
);

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Structure for view `v_current_weak_performance`
--
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `v_current_weak_performance`;

CREATE ALGORITHM=UNDEFINED DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` SQL SECURITY DEFINER VIEW `v_current_weak_performance`  AS SELECT count(`v_recent_order`.`employee_id`) AS `order_count`, coalesce(sum(`v_recent_order`.`order_amount`),0) AS `order_amount` FROM `v_recent_order` WHERE yearweek(`v_recent_order`.`order_date`,1) = yearweek(curdate(),1) ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Structure for view `v_recent_order`
--
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `v_recent_order`;

CREATE ALGORITHM=UNDEFINED DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` SQL SECURITY DEFINER VIEW `v_recent_order`  AS SELECT `orders`.`id` AS `id`, `orders`.`employee_id` AS `employee_id`, `employees`.`name` AS `employee_name`, `employees`.`email` AS `employee_email`, `employees`.`phone` AS `employee_phone`, `offices`.`name` AS `office_name`, `orders`.`order_date` AS `order_date`, `items`.`name` AS `order_item`, `items`.`amount` AS `order_amount`, `clients`.`id` AS `client_id`, `clients`.`name` AS `client_name`, `clients`.`email` AS `client_email`, `clients`.`phone` AS `client_phone` FROM ((((`orders` join `employees` on(`employees`.`id` = `orders`.`employee_id`)) join `offices` on(`offices`.`id` = `employees`.`office_id`)) join `items` on(`items`.`id` = `orders`.`item_id`)) join `clients` on(`clients`.`id` = `orders`.`client_id`)) ORDER BY `orders`.`order_date` DESC ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Structure for view `v_sales_performance`
--
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `v_sales_performance`;

CREATE ALGORITHM=UNDEFINED DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` SQL SECURITY DEFINER VIEW `v_sales_performance`  AS SELECT `employees`.`id` AS `id`, `employees`.`name` AS `name`, (select count(`orders`.`id`) from `orders` where `orders`.`employee_id` = `employees`.`id`) AS `count` FROM `employees` ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Structure for view `v_total_income`
--
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `v_total_income`;

CREATE ALGORITHM=UNDEFINED DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` SQL SECURITY DEFINER VIEW `v_total_income`  AS SELECT coalesce((select sum(`v_recent_order`.`order_amount`) from `v_recent_order` where month(`v_recent_order`.`order_date`) = month(curdate()) and year(`v_recent_order`.`order_date`) = year(curdate())),0) AS `total_order`, coalesce((select sum(`v_recent_order`.`order_amount`) from `v_recent_order` where month(`v_recent_order`.`order_date`) = month(curdate()) - 1 and year(`v_recent_order`.`order_date`) = year(curdate()) - 1),0) AS `total_order_last_month`, month(curdate()) AS `curr_month`, year(curdate()) AS `curr_year` ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Structure for view `v_total_order`
--
DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `v_total_order`;

CREATE ALGORITHM=UNDEFINED DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` SQL SECURITY DEFINER VIEW `v_total_order`  AS SELECT coalesce((select count(`v_recent_order`.`employee_id`) from `v_recent_order` where month(`v_recent_order`.`order_date`) = month(curdate()) and year(`v_recent_order`.`order_date`) = year(curdate())),0) AS `total_order`, coalesce((select count(`v_recent_order`.`employee_id`) from `v_recent_order` where month(`v_recent_order`.`order_date`) = month(curdate()) - 1 and year(`v_recent_order`.`order_date`) = year(curdate()) - 1),0) AS `total_order_last_month`, month(curdate()) AS `curr_month`, year(curdate()) AS `curr_year` ;

  ADD UNIQUE KEY `password` (`password`);
